[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/printf.[0m[1;92mc:45[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m50[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:size_t [0m[1;35mmg_vsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *buf, size_t len, const char *fmt, va_list *ap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:  struct mg_iobuf io = [0m[1;39m{[0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buf, len, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:  size_t n = [0m[1;35mmg_vxprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmg_putchar_iobuf_static, &io, fmt, ap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mn[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:  return n;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is in the `%e` and `%E` format specifier implementation in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.[0m[1;92mc:317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[39m and mongoose.[0m[1;92mc:820[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m824[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m820[0m[39m**: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` - Allocates only [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes for the temporary [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m824[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` - Incorrectly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m as the buffer size parameter, creating a [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte mismatch[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Insufficient buffer size**: Even if the mismatch is fixed, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minadequate for scientific notation output which requires:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Sign [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + mantissa [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes for [0m[32m"-1.23456789"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes for [0m[32m"-308"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = minimum [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with Correct Implementation[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `%g` and `%f` format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use the correct pattern:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` - Adequate [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` - Uses `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass correct buffer size[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The scientific notation formatting logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain unchanged[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The test expectations in `test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[39m` must continue to pass[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing functionality for other format specifiers must not be affected[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzing harness code in `test/fuzz.c` is NOT modified [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit's the trigger, not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bug[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Changes Required[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: src/fmt.c**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `%e` and `%E` format specifier handler in the `mg_vxprintf` function [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m**: Change buffer declaration from:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m**: Change the `mg_dtoa` call from:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: mongoose.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mAmalgamated Source[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply identical changes to the amalgamated source file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m824[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m**: Change buffer declaration from:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m824[0m[39m**: Change the `mg_dtoa` call from:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Optimal Approach**: This fix follows the established pattern used by other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m%g, %f, %d, %u, %x, %X, %p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which all use [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffers and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for the size parameter.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: No changes to the scientific notation calculation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m321[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are needed. The formatting algorithm remains [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical; only the buffer size is corrected.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Addresses the Issues**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates the [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte buffer-size mismatch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m vs [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Provides adequate space for worst-case scientific notation output [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes >>[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m15[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes minimum[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents the stack-buffer-overflow detected by AddressSanitizer[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Stack usage increase**: [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m additional bytes per call [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[39m vs [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible and consistent with other format specifiers.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No functional changes**: Existing tests will pass because the formatting [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic is unchanged.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No performance impact**: Stack allocation overhead is minimal.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Compatibility**: The amalgamated file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmongoose.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is kept in sync with the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodular source.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Similar Solutions**: The codebase already uses this exact pattern consistently[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor all other numeric format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, proving it's the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended design pattern.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Alternative Approaches Were Rejected[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Modifying mg_dtoa or mg_pfn_iobuf_private**: These are utility functions used [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the codebase. Changes could break other functionality.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Removing %e/%E support**: The test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtest/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m expects [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthese specifiers to work, and they are used in production code [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/http.[0m[1;92mc:316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Dynamic allocation**: Would introduce complexity and potential memory leaks. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStatic buffers are the pattern used throughout the printf implementation.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Catching the overflow**: Would hide the root cause. The proper fix is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevention through adequate buffer sizing.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
